    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
             AND [ep].[minor_id] = 0
             AND [ep].[class] = 1
             AND [ep].[name] = N'microsoft_database_tools_support'
    )
